name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 31, 2024
msg:The hotel is located on the edge of Suzhou Bay, next to the Suzhou Bay Grand Theater and the Museum. It takes 5 minutes to walk to the lakeside, or you can ride a shared bicycle around the lake. The scenery is nice.
The hotel service is quite good. If you bring your children to stay, you will get dolls, children's toiletries, and the bed has a baffle. The lake view room has been upgraded. There is an air purifier, smart toilet, and butler service in the room. Good night porridge and milk will be delivered to the room at night. The trash can is also separated into dry and wet. It can be seen that the hotel has worked hard on details and wants to win a good reputation.
The bathroom in the room is very large, and the decoration is in the new Chinese style, simple and atmospheric. The large bathtub is equipped with a disposable cover and an electric towel rail. It is clean and tidy. There are a few sockets in the room. If there are three chargers that need to be charged at the same time, it may not be convenient.
The experience of traveling with children is okay. There is a children's playground, which is not big and has a bit of smell. The ground is covered with ocean balls and artificial granular sand. The sand is too slippery and easy to fall. Smaller children feel that they will accidentally eat it. It looks a bit like rainbow candy. It is recommended to remove the sand.
Catering: An additional buffet dinner was ordered, and the service was okay. The variety of dishes is OK, not much seafood, BBQ is OK, tuna is too woody, a few crayfish feel dead, and the lobster head is also black, many dishes are spicy, children can't eat much.
The breakfast variety is average, in a high-end hotel, I feel it can only be 60 points. There are few Chinese dim sum, waffles and small cakes in the dessert area are dry and hard, not freshly made, it feels like they have been left for a few days. Tangyuan eggs boiled red bean paste fermented glutinous rice are not bad, but there are no wontons!

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:2-bed Room With Lake View
info:Stayed in May 2024

msg:1
Suzhou Bay Hengli Hotel.
During the May Day holiday, people flocked to the hotel.
The prices of various hotels will rise.
It was a turbulent wave swept by the travel fever.
Decisively gave up all kinds of homestays. Choose a star hotel.
At the same price, in the same floating state, I chose the "service" quality.
If a star hotel meets the five-star rating, the requirements of various hardware and software will have certain specifications and standards, otherwise the star rating will not pass.
Adhering to the principle of "quiet, short opening time, wide view, star service", I locked the Suzhou Bay Hengli Hotel by the East Taihu Lake.
Fortunately, I acted quickly and grabbed a low-priced lake view room of 1,100 per night. On the 2nd, Ctrip became 1,783 per night, and it was not a lake view room.
The favor of "luck" is always so Versailles.

2
Suzhou Bay Hengli Hotel.
Located in Suzhou CBD. Five stars.
Built by the beautiful East Taihu Lake. Hidden among the green mountains and clear waters.
The hotel incorporates new Chinese design into the elegant contemporary interior space, citing the elements emphasized by Chinese gardens - wind, prosperity, water, and joy.
Villeroy & Boch wash basin. Delonghi kettle. Hansgrohe shower.
The toilet is a smart toilet from the Toto Ruisit series worth 14,000 yuan.
The coffee cup is Qianfeng Yue porcelain.
The mattress is from the American Simmons Sweet Dream series, priced at around 13,000 yuan.
NESPRESSO original coffee machine, equipped with vertuo coffee capsules.
The bathtub that won the Red Dot Award from Cavide, priced at 18,000 yuan. (Writing this, I feel that I am a bit of a loss if I don‚Äôt take a bath).
German aliseo hanging mirror and hooks. Eko trash can.
L'Occitane toiletries. Free branded drinks in the mini bar.
The room is equipped with welcome fruit. In the evening, the butler also sent hot milk for good sleep.
The butler here is one butler for each guest. Especially the housekeeper Xiong Yanlin who served me, she was thoughtful, polite, and timely, and all the requests were solved in time.
The whole hotel is equipped with a constant temperature swimming pool. Gym.

3
Early morning in the lake view room.
As the sun shines through the clouds and brightens the sky, the whole Taihu Lake comes into view. It looks like the sea but not the sea. There is no excitement of waves hitting the reefs. The whole lake is as gentle as a baby's smile, healing and beautiful.
The blue sky is sandwiched with white clouds, and the blue lake is the same color as the lake and the sky. The West Mountain in the distance is hazy, like a painting or a dream.
Sit quietly beside the French window.
Hold a steaming coffee.
Look at the lake quietly.
Worth it. These two words fall into my heart. The soul finds a habitat at this moment. What heals me is always an inadvertent moment of surprise.

A good hotel.
It always brings you a beautiful thing.
A Pandora that can be kept in memory forever.
Whenever you think of it, you will say-I woke up in the morning of the hotel that day and saw Taihu Lake, which is so beautiful.

msg:On the third day of the ***** New Year, I brought the elderly and children at home to play in Suzhou Bay. Because the elderly person is in a wheelchair, I chose the Hengli Hotel. It was indeed the right choice. The whole family was full of praises and said that they would definitely stay here again next time they come back. .

Serve:
The hotel service is very good. The young man at the door was very active in helping us open the door, push the wheelchair, and carry the luggage. We asked the front desk when we checked in. He also helped upgrade the elderly room to a lake view room for free. After checking in, the housekeeper Xiong Yanlin immediately added WeChat. During the entire stay She was very enthusiastic to help answer questions, informed the breakfast time in time, asked if she needed good night porridge, and also helped arrange a late check-out. When checking out, she also gave a bag of souvenirs as a thumbs up to the little girl. It is worth mentioning that it is great to provide bath seats for the elderly!

environment:
The hotel is in an excellent location. Just across the crossroads is the Suzhou Bay Grand Theatre, Suzhou Bay Museum, and Suzhou Digital Art Museum. It only takes 5 minutes to walk.

facility:
The hotel facilities are also great. Each room starts at 50 square meters and has an air purifier, De'Longhi kettle and capsule coffee machine, an automatic toilet with a sensor opening lid, and a towel rack, so clothes can be dried quickly after washing. .


health:
As soon as you enter the hotel lobby, you will be greeted by the fresh smell of osmanthus, which the whole family loves. I took my baby to swim in the fitness center on the fifth floor and it was a great experience. The locker room has a shower room, a sauna room, and a dressing table where you can sit and dry your hair. During the Spring Festival, there are very few people in the swimming pool, and there are only two families at the same time. The staff did not neglect because of the small number of people, and they were always doing their duty. .
